[10/10/2019, 10:10:46] â€ª+44Â 7717Â 345724â€¬: Yes that's the same as me, Jooles.  The app is Babylon, the NHS service is GP at Hand (the app can also be used for private health care).  The nearest physical clinics are around Canary Wharf and near Kings Cross for blood tests, poking and prodding. [04/11/2019, 09:33:05] â€ª+44Â 7717Â 345724â€¬: Dungeons and Dragons is the original tabletop role playing game.  Think of it like a choose your own adventure crossed with improv.  You create a character from Tolkienesque species (i.e. I'm dragonborn, Anya's half-Orc, you can also be human) with certain skills.  You can create a whole backstory and personality which determine how you behave in the adventure.  The Dungeon Master is basically the storyteller, explaining where you are, what you see, and the results of your actions.  You use dice to determine if you're successful or unsuccessful in your choices.
